Du lieu NVCSKH duoc danh giatheo user VSA - Tren giao dien nhapdu lieu test nghiepvu, Giam sat sé nhap user NV CSKH tiépnhän cuoc goi test vadanh gia ket qua dat/ khong dat tren cactieu chi gom: + Nghiep vu+Ky nang+ Thai do+ Két thuc cuoc goi(chao KH)+Danh gia chung+ Phan loai nghiepvu + Ghi chu- Muc thóng ke, baocao két qua:- Giam sat chon thoi gian xuat file chi tietcac cuoc goi test.- Chon thoi gian xuatkét qua theo user NVCKSH voi cac cot:</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>- B sung Churc nang (tab) nhap dur lieu két qua danh gia test nghiep vu- Nhap don lé (theo l6)- Import theo file - User DTV theo VSA quan ly - Sua ten thanh yéu cau (quan ly két qua danh gia test nghiep vu)- Bo sung 1 bao cao két qua</td></tr></table>

lapcuoc goilan 1nhungkhong lienlacduoc voi KH,sau 30 phut,he thong sé thiét lap cuoc goi toi KH them O2 lan nura, moi lan cach nhau 30 phut (ké tur lan goi lai dau tien). Nhu vay, KH se nhan dugc toi da O3 cuoc goi lai tir tong dai. Néu sau O3 lan két noi, héthóng van khong lien lac dugc voi KH, Viettel sé tur dong nhan tin thong bao dé moi KH thiétlap lai lich hen Khi KH dat lich hen goi lai thanh cong,hé thong sé thiét lap thong tin dat lich cua KH trongqueue cho (hang doi) theo nguyén tac nhu sau:- Thiét lap cu@c goi trong hang doi theo khung thoi gian ma KH dat lich. Trrong hop 2 cuc goi dat lich cung 1 khung gio thi KH nao dat lichtruoc se duoc thiet lap truoc.- Truong hop cung 1 khung gio, có qua nhiéu lich hen dugc thiét lap, hé thóng goi lan luot.- Néu KH khong chon khoäng gio goi lai, hé thong sé thiét lap thoi gian gan nhat,khi cóAgent ranh sé két noi ngay</td></tr></table>
